CREATE TABLE sensor_status (status_id INT PRIMARY KEY, sensor_id INT, is_active BOOLEAN)

CREATE TABLE sensor_type (type_id INT PRIMARY KEY, type_name VARCHAR(255))

CREATE TABLE sensor_location (sensor_id INT PRIMARY KEY, location VARCHAR(255))</t><s>INSERT INTO sensor_data (sensor_id, value, timestamp) VALUES (1, 25.0, '2021-10-01 12:00:00') ON CONFLICT (sensor_id) DO UPDATE SET value = EXCLUDED.value, timestamp = EXCLUDED.timestamp</s>
